### Message

Supervisor-owned workflow gate: outcome_review.

Intent:
Finish runtime-evidence integrity: baseline anchoring with tests, TDD execution coverage with explicit skipped-with-reason handling, normalized by-era incident rates, poll boundary coverage, Postgres parity receipt coverage, TOON metric emission, runtime failure corrective context, advisory lesson non-authority, and canonical execution/outcome decisions that delegate test verification to the supervisor runtime floor.

Review this gate against the current source artifacts and return a typed dual_agent_outcome.
Use decisions/objections to say whether the gate should accept, revise, or deny.

Runtime TDD test contract:
The supervisor runtime floor will verify that every TDD-named test below appears in supervisor-generated runtime evidence. Include tests/commands covering all of them in outcome.tests. Explicitly skipped tests must carry a recorded pytest skip reason; silently absent tests block the gate.
Use only canonical gate decisions (`accept`, `revise`, or `deny`). Do not return `accept_with_residual`; if test execution needs verification, declare the exact pytest commands/nodeids and let the supervisor runtime floor rerun them.

### Message

ACCEPT outcome_review. Gate state materially changed since R9 (HEAD e2be3c7 vs fb63ba4; new prd sha 9631cf5c/tdd fe8b9c73; TDD contract grew 19->23), so FM-1.3 step-repetition does not apply and advancing is correct. All 23 TDD-named tests resolve to real nodeids (grep-verified, none silently absent); the 4 new tests are non-vacuous and intent-mapped (gate-instruction asserts the runtime TDD contract incl. canonical-only decisions and 'let the supervisor runtime floor rerun them'; tdd-name parser reads ### headers; round-objection preserves runtime probe details fixing FM-2.4 withholding; lesson-injection states advisory non-authority). Postgres parity test skips-with-recorded-reason in the gate env, which the floor credits as skipped not missing. pytest is BLOCKED in this gate env (required_evidence_grade=self_reported, consistent all rounds), so I declare one pytest invocation enumerating all 23 nodeids and delegate execution to the supervisor runtime floor as the authoritative executor.

### Confidence

- value: `0.83`
- source: `claude_code_self_reported`
- rationale: Existence and non-vacuity of all 23 nodeids are directly read-verified, the multi-round blocker (state-unchanged + narrow outcome test command leaving 14 missing) is resolved by the materially changed state plus a declared full-coverage invocation, and PG skip-with-reason is confirmed. Confidence is held below 0.9 only because pytest is blocked in the gate env so I could not independently observe green; final authority rests with the supervisor runtime floor rerun.

### Criteria

- All 23 TDD nodeids resolve to real, non-vacuous tests (verified)
- Declared command covers every nodeid so floor executed-set covers resolved-set (verified by construction)
- PG infra-skip carries a recorded pytest reason so floor credits skip not missing (verified)

- Independent pytest green observed in-gate (NOT met: pytest blocked, delegated to floor)
